<h3 style="text-align:start"><span style="color:#000000"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkred"><strong>瑜伽師地論科句披尋記卷第九十</strong></span></span></span></span></h3>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:#000000"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　彌勒菩薩說</span></span></span><br />
<a name="90p6789"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:#000000"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　唐三藏沙門玄奘奉詔譯</span></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:#000000"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　韓清淨科記</span></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="72882:68784"></a>攝事分中契經事處擇攝第二之二</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　本卷延續卷89，仍為〈攝事分〉中四種擇攝的第二種「處擇攝」的範圍。處擇攝共有二總頌、八別頌。處擇攝的第一個總頌中最初的別頌，是說明「安立」的內容：「安立與差別，愚不愚教授，解脫煩惱業，皆應說應知」，又分為八科，分別是：安立諸受、受的差別、眾生的愚癡、不愚癡相、佛教授眾生的情況、解脫、煩惱、業的作用。此處為長行釋中第八科「廣說業」之第二科「業種類」。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、業種類2　卯一、嗢柁南</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科業種類，說明業的種類，分二科；第一科嗢柁南，以嗢柁南列出頌文。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，嗢柁南曰：</span></strong></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五二與十三　四業為最後</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，嗢柁南說：有五種二業、有十種三業、有一種四業。以下以長行說明業的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、長行2　辰一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科長行，用較長的文字詳細解釋，分二科；第一科標列，將偈頌的內容標示列舉出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="90p6790"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">有二種業，一者、重業，二者、輕業。復有二業，一者、增進業，二者、不增進業。復有二業，一者、故思所造業，二者、非故思所造業。復有二業，一者、定所受業，二者、不定所受業。復有二業，一者、異熟已熟業，二者、異熟未熟業。有三種業，謂善業、不善業、無記業。復有三業，謂順樂受業、順苦受業、順不苦不樂受業。復有三業，謂順現法受業、順生受業、順後受業。復有三業，謂學業、無學業、非學非無學業。復有三業，謂見所斷業、修所斷業、無斷業。復有三業，謂三曲業，即身曲等。復有三業，謂三穢業，即身穢等。復有三業，謂三濁業，即身濁等。復有三業，謂三淨業，即身淨等。復有三業，謂三默然業，即身默然等。有四種業，一、黑黑異熟業；二、白白異熟業；三、黑白黑白異熟業；四、不黑不白無異熟業，能盡諸業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有五種二業：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、重業、輕業：依造業的意樂、加行、對象等三種因緣區分重業或輕業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、增進業或不增進業：依業是否增長區分增進業或不增進業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、故思所造業及非故思所造業：依故思與否區分故思所造業及非故思所造業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、定所受業及不定所受業：依故思所造的輕重業區分定所受業及不定所受業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、異熟已熟業及異熟未熟業：依果報成熟與否區分異熟已熟業及異熟未熟業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有十種三業：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、善業、不善業、無記業：以三性區分善、不善、無記業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、順樂受業、順苦受業、順不苦不樂受業：以受法苦、樂、不苦不樂三性區分三種受業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、順現法受業、順生受業、順後受業：以受果時間在今生、順生、順後生作區分。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、學業、無學業、非學非無學業：以凡聖區分學業、無學業、非學非無學業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、見所斷業、修所斷業、無斷業：以聲聞行者所斷證果位階區分業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、身曲業、語曲業、意曲業：以外道由邪見所起之善不善業區分。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七、身穢業、語穢業、意穢業：由猛利貪瞋所造身語意三種穢業區分。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　八、身濁業、語濁業、意濁業：由猛利癡所起的身語意三種濁業區分。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　九、身淨業、語淨業、意淨業：由身語意所造清淨業區分。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十、身默然業、語默然業、意默然業：由身語意所造默然無言業區分。一切能往涅槃默然無言妙行，名默然業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　最後有一類四種業：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、黑黑異熟業，是非福業，因是黑的、果也是黑的，名黑黑異熟業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、白白異熟業，是不動業，因是白的，如色、無色界定，果也是白的，名白白異熟業，如色無色界天異熟業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、黑白黑白異熟業，欲界人天的福業黑白夾雜，因是黑白的，果也是黑白的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、不黑不白無異熟業，能盡諸業。是聖人的出世間無漏業，能斷盡除去福業、非福業及不動業三種業的種子。下文說此業是出世間諸無漏業，是福、非福、不動業斷對治故。因不是染污的；也不是白的有漏善法；也不是不動業。無異熟業，不再有世間的生死果報。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是以長行展開偈頌的內容。若要對業更進一步的了解可以參考〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷8～9及〈決擇‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷59～60。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、隨釋3　巳一、五種二業5　午一、重業輕業2　未一、舉重因緣2　申一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，各別解釋，分三科；第一科五種二業，說明五種二業，又分五科；第一科重業輕業，以業的輕重分別，又分二科；第一科舉重因緣，舉出成為重業的因緣，又分二科；第一科標列，標示列出三種因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知此中，由三因緣令業成重。一、由意樂故；二、由加行故；三、由田故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當知道這當中，由三種因緣使業成為重業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、由意樂故，指動機的強盛；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、由加行，由實際的行動；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、由田，由造業的對象。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、隨釋3　酉一、由意樂</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著解釋，分三科；第一科由意樂，說明由造業的意樂使令業成重。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由意樂者，謂由猛利纏等所作，於同法者見已歡喜，於彼隨法多隨尋思、多隨伺察。如是名為由意樂故，令業成重。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由意樂方面，是指內心的動機。若是由很猛利的貪瞋癡煩惱現行所造作，「等」字包括善心所，重業當然也通於善業，只要是很強大有力量的惡心或是善心所造作的，便會成為很重的善惡業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　見同法的他人所作便生歡喜，隨喜也會使令自己的業成重。於彼隨法，對於隨順所欲造業的法多隨尋思、多隨伺察；例如欲造殺生業，會一直在內心盤算計畫，隨順欲造的殺業生起很多粗的尋思或細的伺察。由於內心的動機，若作惡是極猛利的煩惱現行，作善是極純淨誠摯的心情，這樣所造的善惡業都會變成很重大。如是名為由造業動機的緣故，使令所造業成重業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂由猛利纏等所作者：貪瞋癡三猛利現行，名猛利纏。等言，等取猛利欲樂應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　貪瞋癡三種煩惱猛利現行名猛利纏，指動機而言。應當了知「等」字，是指猛利強大的欲樂。有動機，又有好樂，想要完成這件事的動力非常強大。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="90p6791"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、由加行</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由加行，說明由加行使令業成重。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由加行者，謂於彼業無間所作、殷重所作、長時積集，又於其中勸他令作，又即於彼稱揚讚歎。如是名為由加行故，令業成重。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由加行方面，加行是指實際的行動。前面說的意樂是針對內心的欲望與好樂，這裡則是以實際採取行動來說。實際行動時，若對於所造的善、惡業，無有間斷的相續而作，並很殷切、慎重認真的長時積集而作，又於其中也勸他人令作，如自己殺生，又勸他人也殺生，這惡業很重；或是自己供養三寶，又勸他人供養三寶，這種善業很強大，並且對於所造的惡業或善業，視為功德處處對他人稱揚讚歎。如是名為由加功用行的緣故，使令善惡業變得很重。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　例如修止觀，若能無間所作、殷重所作、長時積集，也勸他令作，這種善業會很有力量；假如造惡業也是一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉三、由田</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科由田故，田是指造業的對象，說明由造業的對象是恩田或敬田使令業成重。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由田故者，謂諸有情，於己有恩，若住正行及正行果。於彼發起善作、惡作，當知此業說名為重。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　田，有生長義，此處指恩田及敬田。由田方面，是以造業對象來說，指諸多有情對於自己有恩的所緣對象，父母或師長，或是住於正行以及正行果的行者。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈決擇‧聞所成慧地〉卷64列舉出正行有三種：一、於佛寶應修供養承事正行；二、於法寶所應修瑜伽方便正行；三、於僧寶所應修共受財法正行，範圍較廣，泛指入佛門修學聖道能安住在正行裡的人。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷23則主張：「若住正行者，即四向；及正行果者，即四果及佛等。」認為正行是指初果向、二果向、三果向、四果向的行者；正行果是指預流果、一來果、不還果、阿羅漢果及佛，這些都是得到正行聖道果的人。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　父母或師長於己有恩者是恩田，正行與正行果行者是敬田。對恩田或敬田發動善業名善作，發動惡業名惡作。由於所造業對象是恩田或敬田，使令所造的業成為重業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是由意樂、由加行、由田故，使所造的業成重。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在〈決擇‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷60，1971頁裡提到由五因緣，使令業成重，包括：由意樂、由方便、由無治、由邪執、由其事。舉惡業為例，由五因緣，使殺生成重業，反之，由五因緣也可以使善業成重。以下舉殺生為例，說明為什麼業會變重的因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、由意樂，指內心的好樂。內心由猛利的貪欲意樂所作，或是猛利瞋、猛利癡。強大的貪瞋癡煩惱與意樂俱行生起，稱作重殺生。若非很強大的意樂，是不小心誤殺的，不能算重業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、由方便，在造作殺業時，方法上太殘忍，便成為重殺生。這些殺生方便包括內心的歡躍；自作令他作，作前長時思量、蓄積怨恨心才作；作的時候相續無間又很專心認真；或者一下殺了很多種類；或令對方失去依止投靠而後行殺害；或者殺害完全沒有抵抗力的人，這些都是重殺生。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、由無治。如果只有行殺業，不能日日乃至極少時持少分戒，又不能將所賺的錢拿來作福，或者不能時時於恩田敬田處恭敬問訊禮拜，這種業會很重，因為無有對治。作惡時無慚無愧，一點也不懺悔，又沒有成就世間禪定離欲，也未成就無漏的聖道，因於沒有對治，名重殺生。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、由邪執。指殺生時有邪見。如有沙門、婆羅門執著代代殺生祠祀是對的，認為殺羊無罪，羊或雞鴨生來即是要給人吃的，認為這是正法，由此錯誤的邪執也會變成重殺生。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、由其事。如果所殺的對象是大身眾生；或是殺害人；或殺父親、母親；或殺尊敬的人；或是有人來歸投、相信自己，卻將他殺害，也會變成重殺生。若是聖人，初果、二果、三果、四果聖人，或是菩薩、阿羅漢、獨覺、或者是佛，都是不應該殺的。佛是殺不死的，若是惡心出佛身血，也都是重殺生。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　本卷90所說的「由意樂」，與〈決擇‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷60是相通的；「由加行」是通於卷60的「由方便、由無治、由邪執」這三點；「由田故」，則通於卷60的「由其事」。這是佛菩薩的智慧，開合自在，以不同角度來說明重業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、例輕相違</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例輕相違，例舉與重業相反的輕業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">與彼相違，說名為輕。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　與上述重業相違的，由於造業意樂不是很強，造作一次後不再相續、也不隨喜、也不讚歎，或是所緣的對象不是恩田與敬田，這種善惡業是比較輕的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、增進業不增進業2　未一、舉不增進</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科增進業不增進業，說明增長業與不增長業的差別，分二科；第一科舉不增進，舉出不增進業的體相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若業非是明了所作，或夢中作，或由無覆無記所作，</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡說到五種不增進業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、若造業時心中不明了，不是心裡很清楚時所造作的業；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、或是夢中所作的善惡業，是沒有力量的；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、或由無覆無記所作，是指造業時沒有煩惱，無善惡的煩惱覆障，或是捨受相應的無記所作。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》若業非是明了所作者：謂無識別童稚所作應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若業非是明了所作方面，是指心不是在明了識別的情況，譬如不能分辨善惡的幼童，這時所作的業，是不會增長的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或不善作，尋復追悔對治攝受，</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、或是不善作，於造作不善身語業之後，能反省覺得自己錯了，立刻追憶後悔、加以懺悔對治、再攝受正律儀，如此業不會增進。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="90p6792"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》尋復追悔對治攝受者：有尋有伺等地決擇中說：或有暫作，續即還起猛利悔心及厭患心，懇責遠離，正受律儀，令彼微薄，未與果報，便起世間離欲之道，損彼種子；次起出世永斷之道，害彼種子令無有餘。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/60.htm#68808:48306">陵本六十卷四頁4858</a>）此應準釋。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈決擇‧有尋有伺等三地〉說：或有暫時作錯事，立即生起強大的後悔心及厭離犯戒的過患，自己於佛前懇責懺悔，遠離這些不善業。懺悔以後再攝受律儀戒，使令不善所作的業力微少稀薄；在不善業尚未感果前，修習世間離欲的禪定，僅能損害所造業的種子；接著依止世間的禪定修毗鉢舍那，證得出世間的無分別智，方能斷除煩惱種子使令不會現行。如〈決擇‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷60，1973頁所說，此處應準照那裏的解釋理解。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又於一切清淨相續所有諸業，</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、又阿羅漢的色受想行識是清淨無漏的，名清淨相續。其身語意三業，名非黑非白無異熟業，是不增進業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》一切清淨相續所有諸業者：謂阿羅漢相續身中諸漏已盡，是名清淨相續。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　阿羅漢身心當中的愛見煩惱都已斷除，是名清淨相續。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是皆名不增進業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如上所說五種業，皆名不增進業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷9，268頁說十種不增長業是：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、夢所作業，作夢時所造業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、無知所作業，即是「若業非是明了所作」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、無故思所作業，不是故意思惟造作的業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、不利不數所作業，不是很猛利、也不是常常作的業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、狂亂所作業，於精神有問題、愚痴發狂、心識散亂、或是有極大的痛苦煩惱逼迫時所造的業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、失念所作業，失去正念所作的業，這類短暫、偶然失去正念，不是故意造的業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七、非樂欲所作業，不是自己想作的，而是由他人逼迫所作的業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　八、自性無記業，所造的業是屬於無記的，不是善業、也不是惡業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　九、悔所損業，不善業被懺悔力所損害，業力減輕不會再增長。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十、對治所損業，不善業的種子被世間道的禪定所制伏、或被出世間道的聖道斷除。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、翻例增進</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科翻例增進，例舉與不增進相反的增進業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知異此，名增進業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當了知，與上面五種情況相反：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、不是非明了心所作業，而是明了心故思所作業；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、不是夢所作業，而是醒時所作業；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、不是無覆無記所作業，而是由善惡心所作的業；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、於不善業造作後，未尋復追悔對治攝受業；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、不是於一切清淨相續阿羅漢所有諸業，而是凡夫所造的業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這五種業都名增進業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷9， 266頁有提到業增上，是指猛利極重的業，稱為業增上，增上有強大義。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　業增上有六相，包括加行故、串習故、自性故、事故、所治一類故、所治損害故。前四種通於善惡業，第五種屬於惡業，第六種屬於善業，合起來說有六種相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、由加行，如有一類人，有極強大猛利的貪瞋癡纏，或是無貪、無瞋、無癡的加行，精勤用功。由強大的貪瞋癡或善心所發起造作的諸業，名由加行故所造的猛利極重業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、由串習，由不斷的熏習，使業力增強。最初造業稱作親近，進一步是修習，實際去作了，又多多的修習，這樣不斷的常常串習善業或惡業，增上所造的善惡業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、由自性故，每種業的性質有強有弱、有大有小。以語業來說，麤惡語比綺語的罪重；離間語又比麤惡語重；妄語又比離間語重。以身業來說，偷盜比邪淫罪重；殺生又重於偷盜。以意業的貪瞋癡來說，瞋心比貪心罪重；愚癡心又較瞋心的罪重。若以身語意三業的輕重相比，殺盜淫的身三業及妄言兩舌惡口綺語的語四業均是前重於後；若以身語意三種業相較，意業最重，身業最輕。這是以不善業的性質而說。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若以施戒修來說，戒性無罪功德勝於布施；戒與修相較，修定慧比持戒的功德還要殊勝。以聞思修相較，思慧功德勝過聞慧，修慧重於思慧。這是以善業的性質所說。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、由事故，是指所緣的對象。如說這事是佛法僧，或是應該尊重、有道德的對象，修恭敬供養，福報也特別大，令所造的業也成重。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、由所治一類，這是以所對治的惡業來說。是指如有一類人，一直造作種種不善業，不會因為良心不安，又去造一點善業，因此乃至到壽盡時都沒有作過善業，也沒有對治這些惡業，令此不善業極為強大。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、由所治損害故，是指如有一類人，包括修定或者是修無漏慧者，斷除所要對治的種種不善業，修禪定使令不善業不能現行；修無漏的聖道，使不善業的種子永遠斷除，成就離欲清淨。若盡形壽相續對治不善業，乃至能夠離欲清淨，先得世間道的離欲清淨，後得出世間道的離欲清淨，所造的善業也是非常的猛利強大。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、故思造業非故思造業2　未一、舉故思造2　申一、標二種</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科故思造業非故思造業，說明故思所造業及非故思所造業，分二科；第一科舉故思造，舉出故思所造業，又分二科；第一科標二種，標出故思造業有二種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="6451:68815"></a>此中故思所造業者，謂先思量已，隨尋思已，隨伺察已，而有所作。彼或錯亂，或不錯亂。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這其中故思所造業方面，指已先思量過，隨粗略的思索考慮，接著仔細的觀察之後，而有所造作的業。又可依造業時的對象分為或有錯亂、或沒有錯亂的情況。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　值得注意的是，故思所作業有二類，如〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷9說：「順定受業者，謂故思已，若作若增長業。順不定受業者，謂故思已，作而不增長業。」若故意思惟後所造作的是特別重的業，並且不去懺除，能障礙正道，令聖道不能生起，則名業障。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為何會故意去造業，於《大乘阿毘達磨雜集論》卷7說，有五種故思造業（有五種原因）：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、他所教敕：他人教導命令自己作。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、他所勸請：不想作，他人勸導自己去作。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、無所了知：不明白功德過失而造業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、根本執著：內心有極重的貪瞋癡，而去造這種業力。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、顛倒分別：有邪見，因此而造故思業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、別釋相2　酉一、舉其錯亂2　戌一、標相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別釋相，各別解釋錯亂或不錯亂的相貌，分二科；第一科，舉其錯亂，舉出有錯亂的情形，又分二科；第一科標相，標出錯亂的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="90p6793"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">其錯亂者，謂於餘處思欲殺害，或欲劫盜，或欲別離，或欲妄語及欺誑等。如是思已，即以此想別處成辦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　錯亂的情形，例如想殺小王，而錯殺小莊，稱作餘處。如要殺害的道理一樣，若想要劫盜，或想離間、或是說妄語、及欺誑他人等，這樣想以後，所成辦的不是想要傷害的對象，是為錯亂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、料簡</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科料簡，重新簡別重罪。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知此中，由意樂故說名為重，不由事故說名為重。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當知道，由意樂也會成為重罪，不僅由於所緣的對象是敬田或福田，而是由於動機。由於強大猛力的動機想要作殺盜淫妄的事，也會令所造業成為重罪。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》不由事故說名為重者：事謂一一業道各別決定所依處事，或有情數、或非有情數。如有尋有伺地決擇中說應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/59.htm#68821:47966">陵本五十九卷十二頁4827</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在〈決擇‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷59，1961頁中曾說及業道，十不善業道或十善業道，每一種業道都有所緣、所依止的處所與對象，或者是屬於有情的種類（數是種類），如人、牛或狗等；或是無情的種類，如鑽石、汽車等無情物。如〈有尋有伺地〉決擇中所說，應該了知。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處是舉業道中五相的「事」來說的。其餘四相則是：想、欲樂、煩惱、方便究竟。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由事、想、欲樂、煩惱、方便究竟這五相廣建立十惡業道的自性差別。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、事，指造業的對象，是有情或是無情；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、想，是於所緣（造業對象）沒有錯誤或顛倒想；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、欲樂，想要造業的希望心（動機）；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、煩惱，有貪瞋癡的煩惱，即是染汙心，不論是有倒或無倒想，想要作的欲樂都會使業成重；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、方便究竟，將業現行及得究竟歸納成一種。採取實際的行動得到圓滿，名方便究竟。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　舉例而言，殺生等不善業道的五相為：有染汙心、起彼欲樂、即於是處、彼業現行、而得究竟。包括：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、染汙心，有貪瞋癡等染汙心；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、起彼欲樂，生起想殺害等造業的意願；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、即於是處，指造業的對象，如想要殺人或畜生等；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、彼業現行，發起身語二業的行動；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、而得究竟，完成造業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是殺生業道的圓滿自相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　總之，這五個條件，如果其中有一不圓滿，都不是圓滿的業道所攝；圓滿的業道必須具足五相。業的現行，最後需透過實際行動而得究竟圓滿，達到目的。這樣具足五種條件使業道圓滿後，便會墮到三惡道去。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、例不錯亂</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例不錯亂，例說不錯亂的情況。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不錯亂者，當知其相與此相違。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前面說明錯亂，是對造業的對象錯亂，反之，如果造業的對象與自己想像符合，則是不錯亂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、例非故思</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例非故思，例說不是故思所造業的體相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若異此業，是即名為非故思造。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果異於上述的故思業，並不是故意造作的善惡業，是名非故思造。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午四、定受業不定受業</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科定受業不定受業，說明定受業與不定受業的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="6457:68827"></a><a name="943:68827"></a>定受業者，謂故思所造重業。不定受業者，謂故思所造輕業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　定受業方面，是指故思所造的重業，亦作亦增長，沒有懺悔、也沒有對治，決定會受果，甚至不只現法受，來生也會到三惡道去。若經過懺悔及對治，業可以轉成不定受，或是不會障礙聖道，也不會到三惡道去，而使重罪輕受，現法即領受了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　大乘佛法中說定業可轉，道理亦同，定業若經過懺悔、對治，在沒有受果報以前是可以轉變的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不定受業，是故思所造的輕業，所造業若十分輕微，或是作了不增長，造業之後並沒有繼續尋伺、造作，也稱作故思所造的輕業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡說故思所造業是簡說，若詳細的說，故思所造業有很多種情況，情況不同，有定受業，有不定受業。義同〈本地分‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷9所釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午五、異熟已熟業異熟未熟業2　未一、標體性</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科異熟已熟業異熟未熟業，說明異熟已熟業及異熟未熟業的差別，分二科，第一科標體性，標示出此二種業的體性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="90p6794"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">異熟已熟業者，謂已與果業。異熟未熟業者，與此相違。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　異熟已熟業方面，是指果報已經成熟的已與果業。例如說造了能感得人身的業，現在已感得人身，便是異熟已熟業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　異熟未熟業，則由於所造業因尚未成熟現前，因此名異熟未熟業，與異熟已熟業相違。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、辨為障3　申一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨為障，說明果報已熟、以及未熟的障礙，分三科；第一科標，標出差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="929:68832"></a>若欲證得阿羅漢時，先所造作決定受業，由異熟果現在前故，能為障礙，不由隨逐身相續故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若將要成就阿羅漢果時，過去生所造的決定受業，由於異熟果現前的緣故，能障礙成就阿羅漢果，而不是由隨逐於身的種子障礙阿羅漢果。一旦果報現前便會成為障礙。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所以者何？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼這樣說？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、釋2　酉一、能為障礙</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科能為障礙，說明能為障礙的情況。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">但由彼業生不平等所依身故，能為障礙，令不能得阿羅漢果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於過去所造的不善業，使得這一生所依的色身不平等，或六根不具足，障礙修學聖道，不能得阿羅漢果。然而業若仍是種子狀態則不能障礙，只有是現行時，如六根不具足或意根被破壞，便會障礙得阿羅漢果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、不能為障2　戌一、標定受</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不能為障，說明不能為障的情況，分二科；第一科標定受，標出不障阿羅漢果的定受業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若無生受，而有後受，於所證得阿羅漢果不能為障，然彼非不是定受業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　定業有很多種，有順現受、順生受、順後受。若為順生受及順後受業，是下一生或下下一生以後才受的果報，相對於今生所證的阿羅漢果來說不能為障，但也不能說這不是定受業，這仍屬定業，只是受果的時間晚一點。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、釋所以</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋所以，解釋它的原因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何以故？由即依彼煩惱助伴，及即依彼諸行相續，施設此業為定受故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是什麼原因？依止定受業而言，由於會造業是依於有煩惱為助伴，以及依五蘊諸行相續，得到生雜染的色受想行識，因此施設此業為定受故，這樣的業稱作定業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若成就阿羅漢果，由於沒有煩惱現行幫助業感果使令諸行相續，故雖是定業但不會障礙阿羅漢。由此可知，若前生造作障礙證得阿羅漢果的業，於今生果報已經現前，如身體有殘缺無法修聖道，會障礙行者不能得阿羅漢果；然而若是下一生或下下一生，不是今生，今生身體沒有殘缺不全，則不成障礙。由於這種業雖是順後受的定業，但此定業必須要有煩惱滋潤，才會有下一生的果報現起，由此定義也說它是定業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》中說：「景師云，欲證羅漢時，先所造作決定受業由異熟果現在前，故能為障礙等者。如凡夫學人身中為障之業如海若山，謂感女身業、欝單越、無想天、黃門等業。此業要生果現前，方能為障不得羅漢，即名業障報障。若未引果者，不能為障。」凡夫甚至有學聖者，在果報體當中還有許多障礙聖者的業，這些業多到像海那麼深廣，像山那麼高大，是哪些業？其中舉出如說感女身業，女身的業較難證得聖道，及北欝單越（北俱盧洲）、無想天，或者黃門等業果（陰陽人等類），也會障礙聖道。但是這些要果報現前才能障礙得阿羅漢，因此稱作報障。若是還未引果報現前的種子狀態，則不能成障。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="90p6795"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由即依彼煩惱助伴等者：此中義顯，彼後受業，若有煩惱助伴，及彼諸行相續，當知非不定受。諸阿羅漢由對治力，雖有彼業，轉令不受，由是施設不能為障，以彼煩惱助伴已永盡故，諸行相續已清淨故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這其中的道理顯示，順後受的業，如果有煩惱為助伴，以及由順後受業感得五蘊諸行相續，應當了知這種業不屬於不定受，而是定受業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　諸阿羅漢由於已有聖道力對治煩惱，雖然有過去生所造的業種子，由於有明相應觸所生受，愛煩惱不再生起，使過去生所造的業種子沒有因緣感果，因此施設順後受的定業，不能障礙阿羅漢，因為阿羅漢煩惱已永遠斷盡，證得盡智、無生智，沒有煩惱使順後受的定業成熟，諸行相續已清淨，將來不會再有一個生命體出現。既然能證得阿羅漢果，可證知此種業不能成障，因此順後受的定業是不能障礙得阿羅漢果的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、十種三業10　午一、善不善無記業3　未一、善業</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科十種三業，說明十種三業的體相，分十科；第一科善不善無記業，解釋第一種三業，善業、不善業、及無記業，又分三科；第一科善業，說明由二因緣建立世間出世間善業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，由二因緣建立善業。一、取愛果故；二、於所緣境如實遍知，及彼果故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，由二因緣建立善業：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、取愛果故。行者發善心，造作善業，將來可以得到人天的可愛果報，如過去生修了五戒的善業，可以得到人天可愛的果報；這是世間有漏善業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、於所緣境如實遍知，及彼果故。行者對於內心所緣慮的境界，包括身、受、心、法，或是有情世間、器世間、或是六根緣六塵時，有善巧的智慧，能夠周遍了知所緣境無常、苦、空、無我的真實相，斷除煩惱，證得聖道果；這是出世間無漏善業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於所緣境如實遍知等者：諸所知事及所知義，名所緣境。於此一切能正了知，是名如實遍知。由遍知故，證煩惱斷及功德法，說名彼果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一切所知事及所知義，都名為所緣境。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　眾多所知事都是阿賴耶識所變現有實體性的因緣生法，以所緣緣來說，這是疏所緣緣，如眼所見的花、桌子、燈、人等事物，都是由阿賴耶識的種子所變現，具有實際功能的諸所知事。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所知義是第六識透過前五識緣慮色聲香味觸時，內心出現的影像，是影像境，這是親所緣緣，是第六識所變現的。譬如看到花時，實際的花稱作所知事，內心現出花的影像稱為所知義。又譬如緣慮某甲時，某甲的色受想行識五蘊稱作所知事，能緣慮的人內心所顯現出某甲的影像，稱作所知義。所緣境的範圍很廣，包括一切有情世間及器世間等。或者說所知事是由前五識相應的所知，所知義是由第六識所緣的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於所知事及所知義，行者能由聞思修、戒定慧得到正確的見解，周遍了知有情世間及器世間一切因緣所生法，都是如幻如化、無常、苦、空、無我，是名如實遍知。由於如實了知所緣境的真實相，行者的身、語、意業不再執著諸所知事、所知義是真實有，斷除愛見煩惱，證得初果乃至阿羅漢果的功德法，說名彼果，此以聲聞乘而言。出世間的善法是需要學習佛法，才能了知及實踐。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、不善業</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不善業，由二因緣建立不善業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由二因緣立不善業。一、取非愛果故；二、於所緣境邪執著故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由二因緣安立不善業，造作與貪、瞋、癡煩惱雜染相應的業，有二種特性：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、能取得不可愛的果報，與煩惱相應的因緣所發動的業行，能取得不可愛果報，名不善業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、於所緣境有不正確、邪曲執著的不善業。行者不明白所緣境是無常、苦、空、無我，錯誤執著我見、常見、斷見、戒禁取見、六十二見等，由於錯誤的見解和思想，執著所緣境為真實有，所發動邪身、語、意行，稱作不善業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、無記業</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科無記業，所造的業不能記別是善或不善。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於善不善二種行相不可記故，立無記業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所造的業不能記別是善或是不善，稱作無記業。無記業有很多種：有異熟無記、威儀無記、工巧無記、變化無記。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是第一種三業：善業、不善業、及無記業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、順樂受等業2　未一、約總報辨3　申一、順樂受業</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科順樂受等業，第二種三業，以受來分別業，說明順樂受、順苦受、順不苦不樂受等業，分二科；第一科約總報辨，以總果報分別，又分三科；第一科順樂受業，說明順樂受業的體相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">順樂受業者，謂初、二、三靜慮地繫及欲界繫所有善業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　順樂受業方面，是繫屬初靜慮、第二靜慮、第三靜慮地的不動業及欲界繫所有福業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有情的樂受可從總異熟果所生、或別業所感現緣所生，此處先以總報說明。若造作初靜慮、第二靜慮、第三靜慮地的不動業，所感初靜慮地、第二靜慮地異熟能領喜、樂二受，第三靜慮地異熟能領樂受，故名順樂受業。福業，包括感善趣異熟，及順五趣受善業。此處指造感欲界人天善趣異熟的福業，依此異熟能領納人天的樂受，故名順樂受業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="90p6796"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、順苦受業</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科順苦受業，說明順苦受業的體相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">順苦受業者，謂能招感惡趣生業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　順苦受業方面，是指造作能招感地獄、餓鬼、畜生三惡趣總報的非福業，依此地獄、餓鬼、畜生三惡趣總報異熟能領苦受，名順苦受業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、順不苦不樂受業</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科順不苦不樂受業，說明順不苦不樂受業的體相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">順不苦不樂受業者，謂第四靜慮及上地等諸所有業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　順不苦不樂受業方面，是造作能招感第四靜慮地及空無邊處、識無邊處、無所有處、非想非非想處諸地總報的不動業，依此第四靜慮及上地無色界異熟能領不苦不樂受，故名順不苦不樂受業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、約別報辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約別報辨，以別報來辨明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">生於餓鬼及傍生中，先業為因感得樂受，當知此業亦得名為順樂受業。唯除那落迦，於所餘處，當知皆得苦樂雜受，即由彼業增上力故，令此依身苦樂雜住不相妨礙。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　總報與別報又名總果別果。即由各有情自所造的業牽引感得四生、五趣等異熟之總體，稱為總報；由各有情滿業力所感受之異熟生各不相同，例如肢體、諸根等各自有別，稱為別報。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如生到餓鬼及傍生中，因為過去造了善業，隨各人業力，有部分的樂受，這種業也可以稱作順樂受業，如畜生道中掛瓔珞的大象，世間寵物貓、狗等，鬼道中的福德鬼、大力鬼等，是由別業所說的。除了那落迦，由於造太重的惡業，於地獄唯苦無樂。於其餘的處所，如欲界的人、天、餓鬼、傍生等，有些福報差，苦受多，有些福報大，苦樂雜受，由於過去所造業的增上力量，使令有情得到種種別報，有時苦，有時樂，苦樂相雜不相妨礙。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、順現受等業3　未一、順現法受業</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科順現受等業，第三種三業，依異熟業受報的時間先後順序說明順現受等業，分三科；第一科順現法受業，說明順現法受業的體相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">順現法受業者，謂由如是相狀意樂所作諸業；若由如是相狀加行，謂事加行、或身加行、或語加行所作諸業；若由如是相狀良田所作諸業；於現法中異熟成熟，如是名為順現法受業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　順現法受業方面，今生由於有強大的欲望，極為好樂的意樂所造作的諸業；若由如是相狀加行，包括事加行、或經由身、語的加行時，具足無間、殷重、相續、勸他、隨喜所造作的諸業；或所造業對象是重大的，如：恩田、敬田；由是因緣在現法中會有異熟果報成熟，名為順現法受業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、順生受業</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科順生受業，說明順生受業的體相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="90p6797"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="929:68863"></a>若所作業，於現法中異熟未熟，於次生中當生異熟，如是名為順生受業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若身語意三業所造的善不善業，在現在的生命體當中果報尚未成熟，於下一生無間將會變異成熟，名為順生受業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、順後受業</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科順後受業，說明順後受業的體相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若所作業，現法、次生異熟未熟，從此已後異熟方熟，當知是名順後受業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若今生所造的身語意三業，在現法、次生的色受想行識果報沒有成熟，第三生以後才得到變異成熟的業，名順後受業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午四、有學等業3　未一、有學業</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科有學等業，第四種三業，以凡夫與聖人來分別說明有學等三種業，分三科；第一科有學業，說明有學業的體相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">有學業者，謂聖弟子，於時時間依增上戒、依增上心、依增上慧修學無漏，及此後得善有漏業，名有學業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有學業方面，是指聖弟子，包括初果、二果、三果聖人，於時時間依增上戒、依增上心、依增上慧修學無漏的聖道成就根本智，及此後得善有漏業的後得智，於日常生活中觸境造業時，由於俱生起的煩惱未完全斷除，但已將感得三惡道的業全部斷除，其所造作的業一定是善有漏業，因此有學的業，包括無漏及有漏二種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、無學業</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科無學業，說明無學業的體相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">無學業者，謂於一切阿羅漢等身相續中隨應諸業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無學業方面，由於阿羅漢將三界一切煩惱種子完全斷除，五蘊身相續中隨所造善法相應的諸業也與無漏相應，是無學業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、非學非無學業</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科非學非無學業，這是指凡夫所造的業，既不是有學業，也不是無學業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此餘諸業，是名非學非無學業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　非學非無學的凡夫業，是指除了前面的有學業與無學業二種以外，其餘在五蘊相續中所造的善、不善、無記業，名非學非無學業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午五、見所斷等業2　未一、出體性3　申一、見所斷</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科見所斷等業，第五種三業，依修行證果過程所斷的煩惱來分別見道、修道、無學道所斷業，分二科；第一科出體性，說明這三種所斷業的體性，又分三科；第一科見所斷，見道位所斷除的業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若見所斷煩惱相應，若此所發思等諸業，一切能往諸惡趣業，此等皆名見所斷業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　見道位所斷煩惱，即分別起的薩迦耶見、邊執見、邪見、戒禁取見、見取見、貪、瞋、癡、慢、疑十種煩惱。若思心所與此十種煩惱相應，由此所發思業（意業）及思已業（身業、語業），一切能往三惡趣的十惡業，這類非福業，名為見所斷業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="90p6798"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》若此所發思等諸業者：此中等言，等取思已業。集論中說：何等思業？謂福業、非福業、不動業。何等思已業？謂身業、語業、意業。（集論五卷三頁）此應準知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　「若此所發思等諸業」其中的「等」字，包括思已業。《集論》中說：什麼是思業？是指與思心所相應的業，包括善行的十善業，是福業；由惡心所相應造作的業，是非福業；與色無色界定相應的業，是不動業。什麼是思已業？是指身業、語業、意業。透過身業、語業、意業，來表達內心的想法，所造作出來的業，名思已業。如《集論》卷5，3頁所說，這裡應準照那裏了知。關於思業及思已業，有不同解釋，《俱舍論記》卷13：「思業謂心所思，思即是業，故名思業。思已業謂思所作，身、語二業思之所作，由思已作，名思已業。」</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、修所斷</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科修所斷，修道所斷的是俱生起煩惱相應的業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若修所斷煩惱相應，及此所發思等諸業，如是皆名修所斷業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　修道所斷煩惱，包括欲界俱生起的薩迦耶見、邊執見、貪、恚、慢、無明等六種煩惱，及色、無色界的薩迦耶見、邊執見、貪、慢、無明等十種煩惱。若思心所與此十六種煩惱相應，由此所發思業（意業）及思已業（身業、語業），即人天有漏善業，皆名修道所斷業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、無斷</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種無斷，說明無斷業的體相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">無斷業者，所謂一切有學、無學出世間業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無斷業方面，是指一切有學的出世間法、一切無學相續中所有諸法包括世間善法及出世間法；有學的出世間法，是與無漏、無分別、離戲論的無分別智相應，它是能斷煩惱的出世間無漏戒定慧所成，不應該斷。無學的一切煩惱都已斷除，苦寂靜，煩惱也寂靜，沒有煩惱可斷，名無斷業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、廣除斷4　申一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣除斷，詳細說明除斷不善業的相狀，分四科；第一科標，標出三相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知此中，由三種相，故思所造諸不善業，即於現法作增長已，還復除斷。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當知道這裡所說，由三種相，對於今生故思所造作種種不善業，即於現法造作增長業後，能暫時伏斷或永斷。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等為三？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪三種相？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科列，列出來三種相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、現法斷故；二、生斷故；三、後斷故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、現法斷故。未離欲凡夫對現法所造不善的增長業，由慚愧心能對煩惱及所造業生起厭離，只能暫時伏斷，使令不再增長，但是不能斷業種子，不能令一向不造。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、生斷故。已離欲凡夫今生離欲，下一生不會到欲界受生，但不能斷除下下生以後的異熟果。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、後斷故。證得三果的聖人，不再回到欲界受生，不但今生不造不善業，於來生也永不再造作欲不善業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="90p6799"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申四、釋3　酉一、現法斷2　戌一、標類</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科釋，解釋現法斷、生斷、後斷的差別相，分三科；第一科現法斷，說明現法斷的相貌，又分二科；第一科標類，標出現法斷這一類的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">現法斷者，謂如有一，於現法中故思造業，作增長已尋復厭離，於其所作受厭離故。此是異生未得離欲。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　現法斷方面，是指有一類人在現法中由故思造業，造作後業增長已又厭離所作，對於所造作的業受到慚愧心影響又生起厭離。這類凡夫尚未離欲，煩惱未得到制伏，無法真的除斷，若強大因緣現前時很容易再重造故業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、釋相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋相，解釋第一種人受報的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">住此命終，而未能令於次生位不造彼業、不受異熟，亦未能令於其後位無有是事。於現法中，亦未一向能令不造。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這類凡夫到命終前由於未得禪定，也未得聖道，煩惱種子還在第八識中，不能使令來生不會再造作不善業，不可能不受異熟果報，也不能使令下下一生乃至以後不造不善業、不受異熟。於現法中努力不造惡業，但也只能暫時伏斷，不能令一向不造。例如：有人一向好賭，經由他人規勸或受到良心譴責，能暫時收手一段時間，由於煩惱很強，誘惑因緣現前，又會再去賭。這是第一種現法斷的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、生斷2　戌一、標類</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科生斷，說明生斷的相貌，分二科；第一科標類，標出生斷種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">生斷故者，謂復有一，受厭離已，雖是異生，而於欲界已得離欲。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　生斷方面，又有一類人，對於欲界諸受已經厭離，雖然還是凡夫，但已離欲界欲。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、釋相</span></strong></span></span></p>
